Really and I mean really rich and innovative Chocalates here. If you have a chocolate addiction I must in good conscience warn you away from this establishment because it is so ridiculously, seductively good but you pay for every bit of that rich goodness. This is not a place where you buy a bag of random candies no this is a place where difficult decisions regarding which one you are taking home with you have to be made. Buying a box here should be a special event but unless you happen to have the money of the upper half of Montereys citizens, do yourself a favor and control your urge. From one Chocalate lover to the rest.< /review>

<Time>1538371933548</Time><Rate>5</Rate>< text>
I come here mainly for the Dole Whip drizzled in Chamoy and sprinkled with Tajin. I always end up staying longer for the irresistible tacos though! I literally eat every taco on the menu during every visit because they are all so good! Sometimes I would order the Chicken Platter served with rice and beans. The chicken is perfectly seasoned and cooked well as the skin is flaky crisp but the meat remains juicy inside.

Taco Al Pastor is absolutely amazing. Slow cooked all day on a stick with Pineapple on top. I can see them slicing the meat and the pineapple as I order topped with cilantro, chopped onions, and chile sauce.

Tacos de Tripas are small perfectly crisp intestines well seasoned and dressed with cilantro, chopped onions, and chile sauce.

Tacos de Pollo is the chicken tacos. It‚Äôs full flavored. Almost as if it was fusion because I can taste chicken pho as I eat my chicken taco served with cilantro, chopped onions, and chile sauce.

Tacos de Asada is juicy tender pieces of steak char grilled to perfection served with cilantro, chopped onions, and chile sauce.

Tacos de Carnitas are moist pieces of shredded pork stuffed with cilantro, chopped onions, and chile sauce.

Tacos de Lengua is my absolute favorite because it melts in my mouth. Perfectly cooked and seasoned topped with cilantro, chopped onions, and chile sauce.

Tacos de Cabeza is the meat around the head of the cow. If you love oxtail then you would love this taco stuffed with cilantro, chopped onions, and chile sauce. I can eat this taco all day if my stomach was big enough.

Tacos de Pescado is their deep fried fish taco. It‚Äôs great because it‚Äôs perfectly seasoned with a battered crunch paired with cabbage, cilantro, chopped onions, and chile sauce.

Tacos de Camaron are succulent little chunks of shrimp. It‚Äôs very tasty and I love biting into the juicy shrimp paired with cabbage, cilantro, chopped onions, and chile sauce.

The best thing is that Oh Wa La Tacos is now serving breakfast. They increased their hours! They now open from 6am to 10pm daily. My new favorite breakfast joint in the heart of Santa Ana every morning where the pancakes are fluffy, the crepes melt in your mouth and the waffles are light and crispy just the way I love it.< /text>

< review>
I had a burrito pollo and used my check-in offer for a free taco de asada. The taco was good. The burrito was good. It was as big as my forearm. They should warn people about that. I'll update my review when I come out from my coma.

2 days later...
Ayer me comi el Plato de Pollo. Ay dios mio! It was so good! A deep fried, split chicken breast served over rice and beans with cheese. It was served with hoisin sauce. I also added another taco pollo and salsa Verde. The chicken may have been fried a little too hard. I'll ask them to prepare it lighter next time. The rice was excellent and the price was right. This place knows what its doing.

The space is large with an open kitchen situated next to the main counter. Another counter with high-top chairs faces the main entrance and a wall of booths is located behind it. Another dining room is located in the back with plenty of seating for larger parties.

The soda machine and extensive condiment station are located aroumd the corner from the main counter with plenty of options including coke and bang; lime wedges, salsa Verde, pickled jalapenos and more.

Everyone around me looked like they were enjoying their food and each other's company. It was great to see.<//review>

< Text>
We've had the need to use storage facilities for business and personal needs over the last decade and the experience has been mixed. We are extremely satisfied with both the facilities and the service at EXTRA SPACE STORAGE. The place is very clean and well managed. From day one, Mathias and his team have provided excellent support and a willingness to "go the extra mile" when necessary. The most recent example is that we were expecting a delivery of two pallets of materials for an event the next day. The freight company told us to be available between noon and 4:00 p.m and that they would call us one hour before delivery. (We work just 10 minutes away.) We were in meetings all morning with phones off and at 11:45 picked up a message the trucker left at 10:30 a.m. saying he was pulling around the corner NOW.

We zoomed across town from the client site and arrived to find that not only had Mathias received the shipment for us, he put it in our unit! That, folks, is exceptional service. No storage facility has ever done that for us! (Let us again say: "Thank you, Mathias, for saving our butts! The Paulaner is coming!")

In addition to the extraordinary, the day-to-day is pretty great too. The facility is clean, easy to use and very conveniently located. We are extremely pleased with EXTRA SPACE STORAGE and plan to have a "home" there for our business for the foreseeable future.< /Text>

<time>1463713017199<//time><name>Sergey Yavnyi<//name><Review>The staff is helpful, and this place has an amazing 4.9 stars (they heavily solicit the customers to write a review so I guess that's why). But my experience with Extra Space Storage has been rather disappointing.

The security measures are mediocre at best. The doors are plywood, and the unit I rented didn't have an actual ceiling, instead it had a metal wireframe. The video surveillance does not cover all of the units. A considerable part of the customers are homeless, and some even have mental health or drug problems. All of this combined makes it for a rather risky place to store valuables.

The representative who helped me admitted that there have been two burglaries in the last three months.

< text>
Listen here, for anyone that's a little nervous or overwhelmed by the whole self-storage thing; I URGE you to use these guys! I recently rented an 8x13' space to store belongings from a 1bd apt, while I was inbetween apartments. Mike helped me out and he was absolutely amazing! Talked me through the whole process carefully, sorted me with a lock, and answered all my questions.
They have alarms set up on all the storage lockers, so you need to 'check-in' via keycode every time you arrive and open the locker. This provided me with great ease-of-mind that my stuff would be safe.
Their access hours are also one of the best in the city.
I ended up stopping my service earlier than expected as I found an apartment quickly; there were no hidden charges or problems cancelling before the next deposit was due.
Honestly; they provided a really great, honest service and I couldn't recommend them highly enough. To that point; I NEVER write online reviews, however it was the great service that made me want to share this. Thanks Mike and team</text>

Dealing with out-of-appt storage is never fun. But if you HAVE to, go to Ext Storage at 1400 Folsom. I needed to get a bigger unit, having piled in the crated art for 8 years....and figured it would be a drawn-out hassle of 2, 3 weeks. So--what I feared would be a long, pain-in-the-butt project turned into a simple after-work task, easily accomplished. Thanks to Ms. Luna.</Review>
